## <a name="adam"></a><span data-ttu-id="afb31-707">ADAM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="afb31-707">ADAM</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="afb31-708">Attributes (Attributi)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="afb31-708">Attributes</span></span>](#adam-attributes)
